msg:Christian's Hotel has the best service I have experienced at any hotel anywhere in the world. The staff were universally outstanding. It was impossible to single out any one staff member for special praise as they were all excellent. We felt like welcomed friends all the time.
The cleanliness and design of the hotel are also of the highest quality.
The only 'negatives' I have are that there is no lobby bar. The restaurant on the 18th floor gives great views. Surely a small section of the restaurant could be converted to provide a lobby bar? The location is also nothing great. There's nothing wrong with the location, there's just nothing great about it either. It's near a subway station, so getting to attrractions is easy, but there's nothing much in the area around the hotel, no great places to eat, no attractions to take a morning or evening walk to.
Those aside, we would 100% definitely stay there again.

Continue to feel the cultural a**osphere of Luoyang, the ancient capital of thirteen dynasties/the land of China...
1) Location: Located in the core business center of Xigong District, the hotel is only about 10 minutes away from the Jiefang Road Line 2 Transfer Center (Line 1-2) and 30 minutes from the train station. It is very convenient to catch delicious food in the surrounding area.
2) Environment: It is biased toward young-style fast hotels. There are 6 types of decoration styles to choose from (Tang Yun, Circle Mystery, Transparent Era, Roman Holiday, and Walking in the Clouds). The "blind box" type opens the rhythm, with a bright lobby and a glass mirror elevator. , all kinds of furniture and furnishings are relatively simple and fashionable.
3) Hardware (dry goods): This time I stayed at Tang Yun, with a red + dark brown tone, in-room bar, high chair, mini kitchen (excluding heating accessories), refrigerator, air evolver, disinfection cabinet, coffee machine, and Kung Fu tea set , the sanitary area is not equipped with a smart toilet.
4) Service: The service may be weak due to limited conditions (parking at the door). After entering the store, you are greeted politely, paying great attention to customer needs, and completely responding to your requests (I have stayed in many hotels and you can definitely get it here üëç), free / The reception service is also very complete.
5) Meals: You can enjoy free fruits, drinks, dairy products and snacks/simple meals every day. The buffet breakfast (Chinese and Western + Japanese) is quite rich. Among the Chinese dishes, the most worth tasting are: 1. Beef soup (optional)üåüüåüüåüüåüüåü, 2. Mutton fried dumplingsüåüüåüüåüüåü, 3. Hong Kong style money bellyüåüüåüüåü .
6) Cost: The software is perfect, the hardware is not perfect, but the price/performance ratio is still good.

msg:The trip to Luoyang was delayed for three years, and the child has changed from being able to squeeze a bed with an adult to having to book a parent-child room. So found Kristin and booked a suite. Read the reviews saying the service is good. that's the truth.
The hotel's facilities are a bit old, and the room decoration style is also outdated, but the overall service does add a lot of points.
The hotel provides free pick-up and drop-off service. We received a text message from the driver when we landed. He waited for us with a sign at the exit. When we got on the bus, there was a hot towel and a fruit snack for each person. I was pleasantly surprised.
When you check in, you can choose fruit snacks on the IPAD, and you can also call and deliver them to the room every day.
Disposable bathtub covers are provided, so you can take a bath freely, and the toiletries are also good. Facial cleanser and mouthwash are also provided, and Shanghai sandalwood soap is also kind to use.
This is the first time I have salmon sashimi for breakfast, the beef soup is also delicious, dumplings, noodles, rice noodles, pancakes and fruits, all can be ordered and delivered to the table. During breakfast, there will be a waiter to ask about the experience of check-in, and any problems can be solved in time. When I had breakfast on the first day, I mentioned the problem that the bedside switch panel was too bright. At that time, I said it was resolved that day, but when I came back at night, I found that it was not resolved. I mentioned it again at breakfast the next day, and it was resolved immediately. I also gave a small gift. Apologies for not addressing the issue in time.
After breakfast, the waiter at the elevator entrance bowed at 90 degrees. I was really flattered and a little embarrassed. In fact, there is no need to bow at such a wide angle, and the staff worked hard.
Let's talk about a few areas for improvement:
1. It may be due to the old equipment, and the bathroom has a peculiar smell.
2. The TV in the bathroom cannot be used for two consecutive days. It should be that the plug is loose, but I can't reach it with my own hands and cannot adjust it. On the first day, I asked the master to look at it, and it was adjusted. When I needed to use it the next day, it was still an old problem, so I didn't bother to ask the master to adjust it again.
3. The lights in the bathroom are motion-sensing. The embarrassing thing is that if you sit on the toilet for a while or take a bath in the bathtub, the lights will turn off after a while, and you have to wave your hand to turn on. Imagine waving while going to the bathroom.
4. When I checked out on the last day, I booked an invoice in advance on the Ctrip order page, but it seemed useless. In the end, I stood at the front desk for about 15 minutes because of the issue of invoicing. On the one hand, the front desk is relatively small. At that time, there were 3 service personnel standing there and it felt crowded. It happened that two or three waves of guests came to check in, and my invoice was scanned twice to get the information, and then it took half a day to wait for the invoice to be sent to the mailbox ( In fact, it was sent to the trash box of the mailbox, but I asked the waiter several times, but the other party was very busy and had no time to respond to me. After asking several times, I finally reminded to look in the spam). During the whole process, because I had to make way for the check-in guests, I was pushed to the side of the counter, and then the waiter was really busy, so no one came to answer me, and the printed accommodation list was also put aside, I again I have to ask for it. It is recommended that the hotel consider expanding the front desk, and separate the check-in and check-out counters, so that the check-out guests cannot feel that the tea is cold before leaving.

Generally speaking, the flaws do not conceal the advantages, and it is the hotel I will choose again, but I hope that the hotel can be further improved, whether it is facilities or services.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Deluxe Double Room
info:Stayed in March 2023
info:Solo travelers
info:6 Reviews
rating:1
posted:Posted March 20, 2023
msg:There are security risks
At around 11 o'clock in the middle of the night, a man opened the door to the wrong room twice. At around 9 o'clock in the morning, a man and his child opened the door to the wrong room. The child was still making loud noises in the corridor. The hotel front desk said that "this has never happened in the hotel." It happened three times within 12 hours. I reported the problem to the director. The director only shouted "yes, yes, yes" and his attitude was extremely perfunctory. In the end, it was so bad that he said, "Ah, if you think we can't solve it, you can call the police." It took three hours to solve it. One thing couldn't be resolved, and the director asked me to stay alone in the room from 9:30 to 2 p.m. on the grounds that "we tried our best to communicate, but the other party was out." I only bullied those I could contact. The assistant to the general manager (surnamed Huang) had a more perfunctory attitude. He repeated the words of the front desk and the manager and director throughout the process and then started laughing without knowing what he was laughing at. Most of the solutions are given by the little girl at the front desk, and the truly powerful management is a bunch of rubbish. The sanitary conditions and infrastructure are pretty good, but the sound insulation is very poor, but the safety issues and the solutions in case of serious problems are worrying. There are many good hotels in Luoyang, so I won't be worried about staying in this one.
